org.pronzato.fabric.client.lab

===== FILE: fabric-lite-services/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/client/lab/LabClientConfig.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.client.lab;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.DiscoveryUrl;
import io.grpc.Context;
import io.grpc.Status;
import io.grpc.stub.StreamObserver;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicInteger;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceClient;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigLineage;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigUpdate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.FabricConfigServiceGrpc;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListConfigsRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListConfigsResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListLayersRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListLayersResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListWorkflowsRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.LineageResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ResolveRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.SubscribeRequest;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class LabClientConfig {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(LabClientConfig.class);

  private LabClientConfig() {}

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    Fabric.Session session = null;
    try {
      // This Java client uses Fabric session plumbing, so caller-app headers are attached
      // automatically. Non-Fabric gRPC clients (C++/Python/etc.) must send those headers
      // themselves on every request when service config uses grpc.identityMode=APP.
      session =
          Fabric.newSession()
              .withGroup("lab")
              .withName("client")
              .withDiscoveryUrls(DiscoveryUrl.URL)
              .withKerberosKeytab(Path.of("vault/kerberos/lenny.keytab"))
              .withKerberosUsername("lenny")
              .build();
      session.start();
      // Non-Fabric clients must use TLS and trust the service CA cert.
      ServiceRunOptions options =
          ServiceRunOptions.builder()
              .withTlsTrustCert(Path.of("vault", "tls", "demo-ca.pem"))
              .build();
      try (ServiceClient client = session.services().client("config", options)) {
        // For raw gRPC clients in APP mode, include metadata headers:
        //   x-fabric-caller-app-group: lab
        //   x-fabric-caller-app-name: client
        // Optional but recommended:
        //   x-fabric-caller-app-instance: any-instance-id
        //   x-fabric-request-id: unique-per-call
        //   x-fabric-trace-id: trace-id
        // Do not send x-fabric-obo-user unless delegated-user flow is explicitly enabled.
        FabricConfigServiceGrpc.FabricConfigServiceBlockingStub blocking =
            client.as(FabricConfigServiceGrpc.FabricConfigServiceBlockingStub.class);
        FabricConfigServiceGrpc.FabricConfigServiceStub async =
            client.as(FabricConfigServiceGrpc.FabricConfigServiceStub.class);

        ListConfigsResponse listed = blocking.listConfigs(ListConfigsRequest.newBuilder().build());
        LOGGER.info("[ConfigClient] listConfigs count={}", listed.getConfigsCount());
        for (var info : listed.getConfigsList()) {
          LOGGER.info(
              "[ConfigClient] config configId={} displayName={} schemaKey={}",
              info.getConfigId(),
              info.getDisplayName(),
              info.getSchemaKey());
        }

        String configId = resolveConfigId(listed);
        if (configId == null) {
          LOGGER.info("[ConfigClient] no configs available, exiting");
          return;
        }

        ListLayersResponse layers =
            blocking.listLayers(ListLayersRequest.newBuilder().setConfigId(configId).build());
        LOGGER.info("[ConfigClient] listLayers configId={} count={}", configId, layers.getLayerIdsCount());
        String layerId = resolveLayerId(layers);
        if (layerId == null) {
          LOGGER.info("[ConfigClient] no layers for configId={}, exiting", configId);
          return;
        }

        LineageResponse resolved =
            blocking.lineage(
                ResolveRequest.newBuilder().setConfigId(configId).setLayerId(layerId).build());
        ConfigLineage lineage = resolved.getLineage();
        LOGGER.info(
            "[ConfigClient] lineage chainValid={} chainDepth={} baseConfigId={} payloadHash={} effectiveTreeHash={}",
            lineage.getChainValid(),
            lineage.getChainDepth(),
            lineage.getBaseConfigId(),
            lineage.getPayloadHash(),
            lineage.getEffectiveTreeHash());

        int workflowCount =
            blocking
                .listWorkflows(ListWorkflowsRequest.newBuilder().setAuditLimit(20).build())
                .getWorkflowsCount();
        LOGGER.info("[ConfigClient] listWorkflows count={}", workflowCount);

        subscribe(async, configId, layerId);
      }
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOGGER.error("[ConfigClient] fatal error", ex);
      throw ex;
    } finally {
      if (session == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      session.close();
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
    }
  }

  private static void subscribe(
      FabricConfigServiceGrpc.FabricConfigServiceStub async, String configId, String layerId)
      throws Exception {
    SubscribeRequest request =
        SubscribeRequest.newBuilder().setConfigId(configId).setLayerId(layerId).build();
    AtomicInteger seen = new AtomicInteger(0);
    CountDownLatch done = new CountDownLatch(1);
    Context.CancellableContext context = Context.current().withCancellation();
    context.run(
        () ->
            async.subscribe(
                request,
                new StreamObserver<>() {
                  @Override
                  public void onNext(ConfigUpdate value) {
                    int index = seen.incrementAndGet();
                    LOGGER.info(
                        "[ConfigClient] subscribe update#{} configId={} layerId={} configVersionId={} updated={}",
                        index,
                        value.getConfigId(),
                        value.getLayerId(),
                        value.getConfigVersionId(),
                        value.hasUpdateTimeUtc() ? value.getUpdateTimeUtc() : null);
                    if (index >= 3) {
                      context.cancel(null);
                    }
                  }

                  @Override
                  public void onError(Throwable throwable) {
                    Status status = Status.fromThrowable(throwable);
                    LOGGER.info("[ConfigClient] subscribe ended status={}", status);
                    done.countDown();
                  }

                  @Override
                  public void onCompleted() {
                    LOGGER.info("[ConfigClient] subscribe completed");
                    done.countDown();
                  }
                }));
    boolean finished = done.await(15, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
    if (!finished) {
      context.cancel(new RuntimeException("subscribe timeout"));
      done.await(2, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
    }
    LOGGER.info("[ConfigClient] subscribe received={} update(s)", seen.get());
  }

  private static String resolveConfigId(ListConfigsResponse listed) {
    if (listed == null || listed.getConfigsCount() == 0) {
      return null;
    }
    for (var info : listed.getConfigsList()) {
      if ("vwap".equals(info.getConfigId())) {
        return info.getConfigId();
      }
    }
    return listed.getConfigs(0).getConfigId();
  }

  private static String resolveLayerId(ListLayersResponse layers) {
    if (layers == null || layers.getLayerIdsCount() == 0) {
      return null;
    }
    List<String> values = layers.getLayerIdsList();
    for (String value : values) {
      if ("algo017".equals(value)) {
        return value;
      }
    }
    return values.get(0);
  }
}



===== FILE: fabric-lite-services/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/client/lab/LabClientConfigRaw.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.client.lab;

import io.grpc.CallOptions;
import io.grpc.Channel;
import io.grpc.ClientCall;
import io.grpc.ClientInterceptor;
import io.grpc.ForwardingClientCall;
import io.grpc.ManagedChannel;
import io.grpc.Metadata;
import io.grpc.MethodDescriptor;
import io.grpc.StatusRuntimeException;
import io.grpc.netty.shaded.io.grpc.netty.GrpcSslContexts;
import io.grpc.netty.shaded.io.grpc.netty.NettyChannelBuilder;
import java.io.File;
import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.FabricConfigServiceGrpc;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListConfigsRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListConfigsResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.LineageResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ResolveRequest;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class LabClientConfigRaw {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(LabClientConfigRaw.class);

  private static final String HOST = "localhost";
  private static final int PORT = 5504;
  private static final String CONFIG_ID = "vwap";
  private static final String LAYER_ID = "algo017";
  private static final File TRUST_CERT = new File("vault/tls/demo-ca.pem");

  private static final String HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP = "x-fabric-caller-app-group";
  private static final String HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME = "x-fabric-caller-app-name";
  private static final String HEADER_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE = "x-fabric-caller-app-instance";
  private static final String HEADER_REQUEST_ID = "x-fabric-request-id";
  private static final String HEADER_TRACE_ID = "x-fabric-trace-id";

  private static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_CALLER_APP_GROUP =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  private static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_CALLER_APP_NAME =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  private static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  private static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_REQUEST_ID =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_REQUEST_ID, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  private static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_TRACE_ID =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_TRACE_ID, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);

  private LabClientConfigRaw() {}

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    if (!TRUST_CERT.isFile()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Missing trust cert: " + TRUST_CERT.getPath());
    }

    ManagedChannel channel =
        NettyChannelBuilder.forAddress(HOST, PORT)
            .sslContext(GrpcSslContexts.forClient().trustManager(TRUST_CERT).build())
            .overrideAuthority(HOST)
            .build();

    try {
      FabricConfigServiceGrpc.FabricConfigServiceBlockingStub blocking =
          FabricConfigServiceGrpc.newBlockingStub(channel).withInterceptors(appHeaders());

      ListConfigsResponse listed = blocking.listConfigs(ListConfigsRequest.newBuilder().build());
      LOGGER.info("[RawConfigClient] listConfigs count={}", listed.getConfigsCount());
      listed
          .getConfigsList()
          .forEach(
              info ->
                  LOGGER.info(
                      "[RawConfigClient] config configId={} displayName={} schemaKey={}",
                      info.getConfigId(),
                      info.getDisplayName(),
                      info.getSchemaKey()));

      LineageResponse resolved =
          blocking.lineage(
              ResolveRequest.newBuilder().setConfigId(CONFIG_ID).setLayerId(LAYER_ID).build());
      LOGGER.info(
          "[RawConfigClient] resolved configId={} layerId={} chainValid={} chainDepth={}",
          CONFIG_ID,
          LAYER_ID,
          resolved.getLineage().getChainValid(),
          resolved.getLineage().getChainDepth());
    } catch (StatusRuntimeException ex) {
      LOGGER.error(
          "[RawConfigClient] gRPC failed code={} description={}",
          ex.getStatus().getCode(),
          ex.getStatus().getDescription(),
          ex);
      throw ex;
    } finally {
      channel.shutdownNow();
      channel.awaitTermination(3, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
    }
  }

  private static ClientInterceptor appHeaders() {
    return new ClientInterceptor() {
      @Override
      public <ReqT, RespT> ClientCall<ReqT, RespT> interceptCall(
          MethodDescriptor<ReqT, RespT> method, CallOptions callOptions, Channel next) {
        ClientCall<ReqT, RespT> delegate = next.newCall(method, callOptions);
        return new ForwardingClientCall.SimpleForwardingClientCall<>(delegate) {
          @Override
          public void start(Listener<RespT> responseListener, Metadata headers) {
            Metadata metadata = headers == null ? new Metadata() : headers;
            metadata.put(KEY_CALLER_APP_GROUP, "lab");
            metadata.put(KEY_CALLER_APP_NAME, "client");
            metadata.put(KEY_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE, "raw");
            metadata.put(KEY_REQUEST_ID, "raw-" + UUID.randomUUID());
            metadata.put(KEY_TRACE_ID, UUID.randomUUID().toString());
            super.start(responseListener, metadata);
          }
        };
      }
    };
  }

}

org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive

===== FILE: fabric-lite-services/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/service/archive/LaunchArchivers.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive;

import org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.configs.ArchiveConfigs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.discovery.ArchiveDiscovery;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.status.ArchiveStatus;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class LaunchArchivers {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(LaunchArchivers.class);

  private LaunchArchivers() {}

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    Thread configs = startArchiver("archive-configs", () -> ArchiveConfigs.main(new String[0]));
    Thread discovery = startArchiver("archive-discovery", () -> ArchiveDiscovery.main(new String[0]));
    Thread status = startArchiver("archive-status", () -> ArchiveStatus.main(new String[0]));

    configs.join();
    discovery.join();
    status.join();
  }

  private static Thread startArchiver(String name, Archiver archiver) {
    Thread thread =
        new Thread(
            () -> {
              try {
                LOGGER.info("[LaunchArchivers] starting {}", name);
                archiver.run();
              } catch (Exception ex) {
                LOGGER.error(
                    "[LaunchArchivers] archiver {} failed: {}",
                    name,
                    ex == null ? "unknown" : ex.getMessage(),
                    ex);
                throw new IllegalStateException("Archiver failed: " + name, ex);
              }
            },
            "launch-" + name);
    thread.setDaemon(false);
    thread.start();
    return thread;
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  private interface Archiver {
    void run() throws Exception;
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.configs

===== FILE: fabric-lite-services/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/service/archive/configs/ArchiveConfigs.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.configs;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.DiscoveryUrl;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.audit.ConfigEventGenerated;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.audit.ConfigEventResolved;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.audit.ConfigEventSubscribed;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.audit.ConfigEventType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.audit.ConfigEventUnsubscribed;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.audit.ConfigEventUpdateCallback;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.IngestManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.IngestTransformer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.SchemaRecord;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.SchemaRecordTransformer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.agent.IngestAgent;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestFormat;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSchemaMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSourceAmpsModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class ArchiveConfigs {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ArchiveConfigs.class);
  private static final String CONFIG_RESOLVED_SNAPSHOT_INGEST = "config_resolved_snapshot";
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();
  private static final boolean SKIP_SOW_REPLAY = false;
  private static final Map<ConfigEventType, EventSchema> EVENT_SCHEMAS = buildEventSchemas();
  private static final IngestTransformer CONFIG_USAGE_TRANSFORMER =
      ArchiveConfigs::transformConfigUsagePayload;

  private ArchiveConfigs() {}

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    boolean verbose = true;
    Path checkpointPath =
        Path.of("data", "checkpoints", "platform", "archive", "configs")
            .toAbsolutePath()
            .normalize();
    CountDownLatch shutdownSignal = new CountDownLatch(1);
    Runtime.getRuntime()
        .addShutdownHook(
            new Thread(
                () -> {
                  LOGGER.info("[ConfigUsageArchive] shutdown requested");
                  shutdownSignal.countDown();
                },
                "configs-archive-shutdown"));

    try (Fabric.Session session =
        Fabric.newSession()
            .withGroup("platform")
            .withName("archive-configs")
            .withDiscoveryUrls(DiscoveryUrl.URL)
            .withKerberosUsername("dfabric")
            .withKerberosKeytab(Path.of("vault/kerberos/dfabric.keytab"))
            .withKekFile(Path.of("vault/keks/platform/dfabric.kek"))
            .withCheckpointPath(checkpointPath)
            .build()) {
      session.start();

      String ampsConnectionName = "amps-fabric-discovery";
      String ampsTopic = DiscoveryTopics.EVENTS_CONFIG;
      List<String> ampsInstances = List.of("instance1", "instance2");
      List<String> ingestNames =
          registerIngests(session.data().direct().ingest(), ampsConnectionName, ampsTopic);
      LOGGER.info(
          "[ConfigUsageArchive] verbose={} checkpointPath={} ingests={}",
          verbose,
          checkpointPath,
          ingestNames);

      IngestManager ingest = session.data().direct().ingest();
      List<IngestAgent> agents = new ArrayList<>();
      try {
        for (String instanceName : ampsInstances) {
          IngestAgent agent =
              ingest.agent(
                  IngestAgent.builder()
                      .withIngestAllowlist(ingestNames)
                      .withIngestRuntimeOptions(
                          IngestManager.IngestRuntimeOptions.builder()
                              .withParquetRollPolicy(20_000, 5_000L)
                              .withAmpsConnectionInstance(instanceName)
                              .withParquetFilenamePrefix(instanceName)
                              .withAmpsLogIncoming(verbose)
                              .withAmpsLogOutgoing(verbose)
                              .withAmpsTransformer(CONFIG_USAGE_TRANSFORMER)
                              .withAmpsPersistOofAsRows(true)
                              .build()));
          agent.start();
          agents.add(agent);

          LOGGER.info(
              "[ConfigUsageArchive] ingests={} instance={} runtimeStarted={}",
              ingestNames,
              instanceName,
              agent.started());
        }

        LOGGER.info(
            "[ConfigUsageArchive] running topic={} connection={} instances={} agents={} stopHint=Ctrl+C",
            ampsTopic,
            ampsConnectionName,
            ampsInstances,
            agents.size());

        while (shutdownSignal.getCount() > 0) {
          shutdownSignal.await(30_000L, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
          if (shutdownSignal.getCount() > 0) {
            int runningCount = 0;
            for (IngestAgent agent : agents) {
              if (agent != null && agent.started()) {
                runningCount++;
              }
            }
            LOGGER.info(
                "[ConfigUsageArchive] heartbeat agentsRunning={} totalAgents={}",
                runningCount,
                agents.size());
          }
        }
      } finally {
        for (IngestAgent agent : agents) {
          if (agent == null) {
            continue;
          }
          try {
            agent.close();
          } catch (Exception error) {
            String message = error == null ? null : error.getMessage();
            LOGGER.warn(
                "[ConfigUsageArchive] agent stop failed message={}",
                message == null ? "unknown" : message);
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }

  private static List<String> registerIngests(
      IngestManager ingest, String ampsConnectionName, String ampsTopic) {
    List<String> names = new ArrayList<>();
    for (ConfigEventType eventType : ConfigEventType.values()) {
      String ingestName = eventType.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      boolean existed = ingest.exists(ingestName);
      ingest.admin().register(modelForEvent(ingestName, eventType, ampsConnectionName, ampsTopic));
      names.add(ingestName);
      LOGGER.info(
          "[ConfigUsageArchive] ingest={} action={} eventType={} ampsConnection={} ampsTopic={}",
          ingestName,
          existed ? "updated" : "registered",
          eventType,
          ampsConnectionName,
          ampsTopic);
    }
    boolean snapshotExisted = ingest.exists(CONFIG_RESOLVED_SNAPSHOT_INGEST);
    ingest
        .admin()
        .register(
            modelForEvent(
                CONFIG_RESOLVED_SNAPSHOT_INGEST,
                ConfigEventType.CONFIG_RESOLVED,
                ampsConnectionName,
                ampsTopic));
    names.add(CONFIG_RESOLVED_SNAPSHOT_INGEST);
    LOGGER.info(
        "[ConfigUsageArchive] ingest={} action={} eventType={} ampsConnection={} ampsTopic={}",
        CONFIG_RESOLVED_SNAPSHOT_INGEST,
        snapshotExisted ? "updated" : "registered",
        ConfigEventType.CONFIG_RESOLVED,
        ampsConnectionName,
        ampsTopic);
    return List.copyOf(names);
  }

  private static IngestModel modelForEvent(
      String ingestName,
      ConfigEventType eventType,
      String ampsConnectionName,
      String ampsTopic) {
    EventSchema eventSchema = EVENT_SCHEMAS.get(eventType);
    if (eventSchema == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Missing schema model for config event type=" + eventType);
    }
    return IngestModel.builder()
        .withName(ingestName)
        .withSchemaMode(IngestSchemaMode.ADD_COLUMNS)
        .withSchema(eventSchema.schema())
        .withSourceAmps(
            source ->
                source
                    .withFormat(IngestFormat.JSON)
                    .withConnectionName(ampsConnectionName)
                    .withTopic(ampsTopic)
                    .withSowSubscribe(false)
                    .withFilter(eventTypeFilter(eventType))
                    .withMode(IngestSourceAmpsModel.Mode.STREAM)
                    .withOofHandling(IngestSourceAmpsModel.OofHandling.DELETE_EVENT))
        .withTargetParquet(target -> target.withConnectionName("s3-fabric"))
        .build();
  }

  private static Map<ConfigEventType, EventSchema> buildEventSchemas() {
    EnumMap<ConfigEventType, EventSchema> schemas = new EnumMap<>(ConfigEventType.class);
    for (ConfigEventType eventType : ConfigEventType.values()) {
      Class<?> eventClass = eventRecordClass(eventType);
      SchemaModel schema =
          SchemaRecord.fromRecord(
              eventClass,
              SchemaRecord.Options.builder()
                  .withGroup("platform")
                  .withName("config-usage-events-" + eventType.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))
                  .withNestingMode(SchemaRecord.NestingMode.JSON)
                  .withSnakeCaseNames(false)
                  .withAppendJsonSuffixForNested(true)
                  .withIncludeAmpsCommand(true)
                  .withIncludeRecordClassName(true)
                  .withIncludePayloadJson(true)
                  .build());
      schemas.put(eventType, new EventSchema(schema, eventClass.getName()));
    }
    return Map.copyOf(schemas);
  }

  private static Class<?> eventRecordClass(ConfigEventType eventType) {
    return switch (eventType) {
      case CONFIG_RESOLVED -> ConfigEventResolved.class;
      case CONFIG_SUBSCRIBED -> ConfigEventSubscribed.class;
      case CONFIG_UPDATE_CALLBACK -> ConfigEventUpdateCallback.class;
      case CONFIG_UNSUBSCRIBED -> ConfigEventUnsubscribed.class;
      case CONFIG_GENERATED -> ConfigEventGenerated.class;
    };
  }

  private static String eventTypeFilter(ConfigEventType eventType) {
    return "/envelope/eventType = '" + eventType.name() + "'";
  }

  private static String transformConfigUsagePayload(String payloadText, Integer ampsCommand) {
    String payload = Strings.requireNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(payloadText), "payloadText");
    try {
      JsonNode root = MAPPER.readTree(payload);
      ConfigEventType eventType = readEventType(root);
      EventSchema eventSchema = eventType == null ? null : EVENT_SCHEMAS.get(eventType);
      SchemaModel schema = eventSchema == null ? null : eventSchema.schema();
      String recordClass = eventSchema == null ? null : eventSchema.recordClassName();
      return SchemaRecordTransformer.transform(
          MAPPER,
          root,
          root,
          payload,
          ampsCommand,
          schema,
          recordClass,
          SKIP_SOW_REPLAY);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to transform config usage payload: "
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(ex.getMessage(), "unknown"),
          ex);
    }
  }

  private static ConfigEventType readEventType(JsonNode root) {
    if (root == null || root.isMissingNode()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode eventType = root.path("envelope").path("eventType");
    if (eventType == null || eventType.isMissingNode() || eventType.isNull()) {
      return null;
    }
    return ConfigEventType.fromJson(eventType.asText(null));
  }

  private record EventSchema(SchemaModel schema, String recordClassName) {}
}



org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.discovery

===== FILE: fabric-lite-services/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/service/archive/discovery/ArchiveDiscovery.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.discovery;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.DiscoveryUrl;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.IngestManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.IngestTransformer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.SchemaRecord;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.SchemaRecordTransformer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.agent.IngestAgent;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestFormat;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSchemaMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSourceAmpsModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class ArchiveDiscovery {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ArchiveDiscovery.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();
  private static final boolean SKIP_SOW_REPLAY = false;
  private static final SchemaModel DISCOVERY_SCHEMA = discoverySchema();
  private static final String DISCOVERY_RECORD_CLASS = DefinitionEnvelope.class.getName();
  private static final IngestTransformer DISCOVERY_TRANSFORMER =
      SchemaRecordTransformer.builder()
          .withMapper(MAPPER)
          .withSchema(DISCOVERY_SCHEMA)
          .withSourceSelector(root -> root.path("envelope"))
          .withRecordClassName(DISCOVERY_RECORD_CLASS)
          .withSkipSowReplay(SKIP_SOW_REPLAY)
          .build();

  private ArchiveDiscovery() {}

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    boolean verbose = args != null && args.length > 0 && Boolean.parseBoolean(args[0]);
    CountDownLatch shutdownSignal = new CountDownLatch(1);
    Runtime.getRuntime()
        .addShutdownHook(
            new Thread(
                () -> {
                  LOGGER.info("[DiscoveryArchive] shutdown requested");
                  shutdownSignal.countDown();
                },
                "discovery-archive-shutdown"));

    try (Fabric.Session session =
        Fabric.newSession()
            .withGroup("platform")
            .withName("archive-discovery")
            .withDiscoveryUrls(DiscoveryUrl.URL)
            .withKerberosUsername("dfabric")
            .withKerberosKeytab(Path.of("vault/kerberos/dfabric.keytab"))
            .withKekFile(Path.of("vault/keks/platform/dfabric.kek"))
            .withCheckpointPath(Path.of("data", "checkpoints", "platform", "archive", "discovery"))
            .build()) {
      session.start();

      String ingestName = "discovery";
      String ampsConnectionName = "amps-fabric-discovery";
      String ampsTopic = DiscoveryTopics.DISCOVERY;

      IngestManager ingest = session.data().direct().ingest();
      IngestAgent agent = null;
      try {
        boolean existed = ingest.exists(ingestName);

        ingest.admin()
            .register(
                IngestModel.builder()
                    .withName(ingestName)
                    .withSchemaMode(IngestSchemaMode.STRICT)
                    .withSchema(DISCOVERY_SCHEMA)
                    .withSourceAmps(
                        source ->
                            source
                                .withFormat(IngestFormat.JSON)
                                .withConnectionName(ampsConnectionName)
                                .withTopic(ampsTopic)
                                .withSowSubscribe(false)
                                .withMode(IngestSourceAmpsModel.Mode.STREAM)
                                .withOofHandling(IngestSourceAmpsModel.OofHandling.DELETE_EVENT))
                    .withTargetParquet(target -> target.withConnectionName("s3-fabric"))
                    .build());

        LOGGER.info(
            "[DiscoveryArchive] ingest={} action={} ampsConnection={} ampsTopic={}",
            ingestName,
            existed ? "updated" : "registered",
            ampsConnectionName,
            ampsTopic);

        IngestManager.IngestRuntimeOptions runtimeOptions =
            IngestManager.IngestRuntimeOptions.builder()
                .withParquetRollPolicy(20_000, 5_000L)
                .withAmpsLogIncoming(verbose)
                .withAmpsLogOutgoing(verbose)
                .withAmpsTransformer(DISCOVERY_TRANSFORMER)
                .withAmpsPersistOofAsRows(true)
                .build();

        agent =
            ingest.agent(
                IngestAgent.builder()
                    .withIngestAllowlist(List.of(ingestName))
                    .withIngestRuntimeOptions(runtimeOptions));
        agent.start();
        LOGGER.info("[DiscoveryArchive] ingest={} agentStarted={}", ingestName, agent.started());

        LOGGER.info(
            "[DiscoveryArchive] running topic={} connection={} stopHint=Ctrl+C",
            ampsTopic,
            ampsConnectionName);

        while (shutdownSignal.getCount() > 0) {
          shutdownSignal.await(30_000L, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
          if (shutdownSignal.getCount() > 0) {
            LOGGER.info(
                "[DiscoveryArchive] heartbeat agentStarted={}", agent != null && agent.started());
          }
        }
      } finally {
        try {
          if (agent != null) {
            agent.close();
          }
        } catch (Exception error) {
          String message = error == null ? null : error.getMessage();
          LOGGER.warn(
              "[DiscoveryArchive] agent stop failed message={}",
              message == null ? "unknown" : message);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  private static SchemaModel discoverySchema() {
    return SchemaRecord.fromRecord(
        DefinitionEnvelope.class,
        SchemaRecord.Options.builder()
            .withGroup("platform")
            .withName("discovery-events")
            .withNestingMode(SchemaRecord.NestingMode.FLATTEN)
            .withIncludeAmpsCommand(true)
            .withIncludeRecordClassName(true)
            .withIncludePayloadJson(true)
            .build());
  }

}



org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.entitlements

===== FILE: fabric-lite-services/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/service/archive/entitlements/ArchiveEntitlements.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.entitlements;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.DiscoveryUrl;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.IngestManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.IngestTransformer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.SchemaRecord;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.SchemaRecordTransformer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.agent.IngestAgent;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestFormat;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSchemaMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSourceAmpsModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events.EntitlementEvent;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class ArchiveEntitlements {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ArchiveEntitlements.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();
  private static final boolean SKIP_SOW_REPLAY = false;
  private static final String ARCHIVE_SESSION_APP = "archive-entitlements";
  private static final String ARCHIVE_DATASET_ID = "dataset:platform/default/entitlements";
  private static final SchemaModel ENTITLEMENT_SCHEMA = entitlementSchema();
  private static final String ENTITLEMENT_RECORD_CLASS = EntitlementEvent.class.getName();
  private static final IngestTransformer ENTITLEMENT_TRANSFORMER =
      SchemaRecordTransformer.builder()
          .withMapper(MAPPER)
          .withSchema(ENTITLEMENT_SCHEMA)
          .withRecordClassName(ENTITLEMENT_RECORD_CLASS)
          .withSkipSowReplay(SKIP_SOW_REPLAY)
          .build();

  private ArchiveEntitlements() {}

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    boolean verbose = true;
    Path checkpointPath =
        Path.of("data", "checkpoints", "platform", "archive", "entitlements")
            .toAbsolutePath()
            .normalize();
    CountDownLatch shutdownSignal = new CountDownLatch(1);
    Runtime.getRuntime()
        .addShutdownHook(
            new Thread(
                () -> {
                  LOGGER.info("[EntitlementsArchive] shutdown requested");
                  shutdownSignal.countDown();
                },
                "entitlements-archive-shutdown"));

    try (Fabric.Session session =
        Fabric.newSession()
            .withGroup("platform")
            .withName("archive-entitlements")
            .withDiscoveryUrls(DiscoveryUrl.URL)
            .withKerberosUsername("dfabric")
            .withKerberosKeytab(Path.of("vault/kerberos/dfabric.keytab"))
            .withKekFile(Path.of("vault/keks/platform/dfabric.kek"))
            .withCheckpointPath(checkpointPath)
            .build()) {
      session.start();

      String ingestName = "entitlements";
      String ampsConnectionName = "amps-fabric-discovery";
      String ampsTopic = DiscoveryTopics.EVENTS_ENTITLEMENTS;
      String ampsFilter = selfEventFilter();
      List<String> ampsInstances = List.of("instance1", "instance2");
      LOGGER.info("[EntitlementsArchive] verbose={} checkpointPath={}", verbose, checkpointPath);

      IngestManager ingest = session.data().direct().ingest();
      List<IngestAgent> agents = new ArrayList<>();
      try {

        boolean existed = ingest.exists(ingestName);

        ingest
            .admin()
            .register(
                IngestModel.builder()
                    .withName(ingestName)
                    .withSchemaMode(IngestSchemaMode.ADD_COLUMNS)
                    .withSchema(ENTITLEMENT_SCHEMA)
                    .withSourceAmps(
                        source ->
                            source
                                .withFormat(IngestFormat.JSON)
                                .withConnectionName(ampsConnectionName)
                                .withTopic(ampsTopic)
                                .withSowSubscribe(false)
                                .withFilter(ampsFilter)
                                .withMode(IngestSourceAmpsModel.Mode.STREAM)
                                .withOofHandling(IngestSourceAmpsModel.OofHandling.DELETE_EVENT))
                    .withTargetParquet(target -> target.withConnectionName("s3-fabric"))
                    .build());

        LOGGER.info(
            "[EntitlementsArchive] ingest={} action={} ampsConnection={} ampsTopic={} filter={}",
            ingestName,
            existed ? "updated" : "registered",
            ampsConnectionName,
            ampsTopic,
            ampsFilter);

        for (String instanceName : ampsInstances) {
          IngestAgent agent =
              ingest.agent(
                  IngestAgent.builder()
                      .withIngestAllowlist(List.of(ingestName))
                      .withIngestRuntimeOptions(
                          IngestManager.IngestRuntimeOptions.builder()
                              .withParquetRollPolicy(20_000, 5_000L)
                              .withAmpsConnectionInstance(instanceName)
                              .withParquetFilenamePrefix(instanceName)
                              .withAmpsLogIncoming(verbose)
                              .withAmpsLogOutgoing(verbose)
                              .withAmpsTransformer(ENTITLEMENT_TRANSFORMER)
                              .withAmpsPersistOofAsRows(true)
                              .build()));
          agent.start();
          agents.add(agent);

          LOGGER.info(
              "[EntitlementsArchive] ingest={} instance={} runtimeStarted={}",
              ingestName,
              instanceName,
              agent.started());
        }

        LOGGER.info(
            "[EntitlementsArchive] running topic={} connection={} instances={} agents={} stopHint=Ctrl+C",
            ampsTopic,
            ampsConnectionName,
            ampsInstances,
            agents.size());
        LOGGER.info(
            "[EntitlementsArchive] note: this example uses one AMPS connection name for both agents; switch per-instance connection names when available.");

        while (shutdownSignal.getCount() > 0) {
          shutdownSignal.await(30_000L, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
          if (shutdownSignal.getCount() > 0) {
            int runningCount = 0;
            for (IngestAgent agent : agents) {
              if (agent != null && agent.started()) {
                runningCount++;
              }
            }
            LOGGER.info(
                "[EntitlementsArchive] heartbeat agentsRunning={} totalAgents={}",
                runningCount,
                agents.size());
          }
        }
      } finally {
        for (IngestAgent agent : agents) {
          if (agent == null) {
            continue;
          }
          try {
            agent.close();
          } catch (Exception error) {
            String message = error == null ? null : error.getMessage();
            LOGGER.warn(
                "[EntitlementsArchive] agent stop failed message={}",
                message == null ? "unknown" : message);
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }

  private static SchemaModel entitlementSchema() {
    return SchemaRecord.fromRecord(
        EntitlementEvent.class,
        SchemaRecord.Options.builder()
            .withGroup("platform")
            .withName("entitlement-events")
            .withSnakeCaseNames(false)
            .withIncludeAmpsCommand(true)
            .withIncludeRecordClassName(true)
            .withIncludePayloadJson(true)
            .build());
  }

  private static String selfEventFilter() {
    return "/sessionApp != '"
        + ARCHIVE_SESSION_APP
        + "' and /resourceId != '"
        + ARCHIVE_DATASET_ID
        + "'";
  }

}



org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.status

package org.pronzato.fabric.service.archive.status;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.DiscoveryUrl;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.IngestManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.IngestTransformer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.SchemaRecord;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.SchemaRecordTransformer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.agent.IngestAgent;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestFormat;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSchemaMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSourceAmpsModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class ArchiveStatus {

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ArchiveStatus.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();
  private static final boolean SKIP_SOW_REPLAY = false;
  private static final SchemaModel STATUS_APP_SCHEMA = statusAppSchema();
  private static final SchemaModel STATUS_SERVICE_SCHEMA = statusServiceSchema();
  private static final String STATUS_APP_RECORD_CLASS = DefinitionStatusApp.class.getName();
  private static final String STATUS_SERVICE_RECORD_CLASS = DefinitionStatusService.class.getName();
  private static final String STATUS_APP_FILTER = "/type = 'STATUS_APP' and /state != 'RUNNING'";
  private static final IngestTransformer STATUS_TRANSFORMER = ArchiveStatus::transformStatusPayload;

  private ArchiveStatus() {}

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    boolean verbose = true;
    CountDownLatch shutdownSignal = new CountDownLatch(1);
    Runtime.getRuntime()
        .addShutdownHook(
            new Thread(
                () -> {
                  LOGGER.info("[StatusArchive] shutdown requested");
                  shutdownSignal.countDown();
                },
                "status-archive-shutdown"));

    try (Fabric.Session session =
        Fabric.newSession()
            .withGroup("platform")
            .withName("archive-status")
            .withDiscoveryUrls(DiscoveryUrl.URL)
            .withKerberosUsername("dfabric")
            .withKerberosKeytab(Path.of("vault/kerberos/dfabric.keytab"))
            .withKekFile(Path.of("vault/keks/platform/dfabric.kek"))
            .withCheckpointPath(Path.of("data", "checkpoints", "platform", "archive", "status"))
            .build()) {
      session.start();

      String ampsConnectionName = "amps-fabric-discovery";
      String ampsTopic = DiscoveryTopics.STATUS;
      List<String> ingestNames =
          registerIngests(session.data().direct().ingest(), ampsConnectionName, ampsTopic);

      IngestManager ingest = session.data().direct().ingest();
      IngestAgent agent = null;
      try {
        IngestManager.IngestRuntimeOptions runtimeOptions =
            IngestManager.IngestRuntimeOptions.builder()
                .withParquetRollPolicy(20_000, 5_000L)
                .withAmpsLogIncoming(verbose)
                .withAmpsLogOutgoing(verbose)
                .withAmpsTransformer(STATUS_TRANSFORMER)
                .withAmpsPersistOofAsRows(true)
                .build();

        agent =
            ingest.agent(
                IngestAgent.builder()
                    .withIngestAllowlist(ingestNames)
                    .withIngestRuntimeOptions(runtimeOptions));
        agent.start();
        LOGGER.info(
            "[StatusArchive] ingests={} agentStarted={}",
            ingestNames,
            agent.started());

        LOGGER.info(
            "[StatusArchive] running topic={} connection={} ingests={} stopHint=Ctrl+C",
            ampsTopic,
            ampsConnectionName,
            ingestNames);

        while (shutdownSignal.getCount() > 0) {
          shutdownSignal.await(30_000L, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
          if (shutdownSignal.getCount() > 0) {
            LOGGER.info("[StatusArchive] heartbeat agentStarted={}", agent != null && agent.started());
          }
        }
      } finally {
        try {
          if (agent != null) {
            agent.close();
          }
        } catch (Exception error) {
          String message = error == null ? null : error.getMessage();
          LOGGER.warn(
              "[StatusArchive] agent stop failed message={}",
              message == null ? "unknown" : message);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  private static List<String> registerIngests(
      IngestManager ingest, String ampsConnectionName, String ampsTopic) {
    List<String> names = new ArrayList<>();
    names.add(registerStatusAppIngest(ingest, ampsConnectionName, ampsTopic));
    names.add(registerStatusServiceIngest(ingest, ampsConnectionName, ampsTopic));
    return List.copyOf(names);
  }

  private static String registerStatusAppIngest(
      IngestManager ingest, String ampsConnectionName, String ampsTopic) {
    String ingestName = "status_app";
    boolean existed = ingest.exists(ingestName);
    ingest
        .admin()
        .register(
            IngestModel.builder()
                .withName(ingestName)
                .withSchemaMode(IngestSchemaMode.ADD_COLUMNS)
                .withSchema(STATUS_APP_SCHEMA)
                .withSourceAmps(
                    source ->
                        source
                            .withFormat(IngestFormat.JSON)
                            .withConnectionName(ampsConnectionName)
                            .withTopic(ampsTopic)
                            .withSowSubscribe(true)
                            .withFilter(STATUS_APP_FILTER)
                            .withMode(IngestSourceAmpsModel.Mode.STREAM)
                            .withOofHandling(IngestSourceAmpsModel.OofHandling.DELETE_EVENT))
                .withTargetParquet(target -> target.withConnectionName("s3-fabric"))
                .build());
    LOGGER.info(
        "[StatusArchive] ingest={} action={} ampsConnection={} ampsTopic={} filter={}",
        ingestName,
        existed ? "updated" : "registered",
        ampsConnectionName,
        ampsTopic,
        STATUS_APP_FILTER);
    return ingestName;
  }

  private static String registerStatusServiceIngest(
      IngestManager ingest, String ampsConnectionName, String ampsTopic) {
    String ingestName = "status_service";
    boolean existed = ingest.exists(ingestName);
    ingest
        .admin()
        .register(
            IngestModel.builder()
                .withName(ingestName)
                .withSchemaMode(IngestSchemaMode.ADD_COLUMNS)
                .withSchema(STATUS_SERVICE_SCHEMA)
                .withSourceAmps(
                    source ->
                        source
                            .withFormat(IngestFormat.JSON)
                            .withConnectionName(ampsConnectionName)
                            .withTopic(ampsTopic)
                            .withSowSubscribe(true)
                            .withFilter("/type = 'STATUS_SERVICE'")
                            .withMode(IngestSourceAmpsModel.Mode.STREAM)
                            .withOofHandling(IngestSourceAmpsModel.OofHandling.DELETE_EVENT))
                .withTargetParquet(target -> target.withConnectionName("s3-fabric"))
                .build());
    LOGGER.info(
        "[StatusArchive] ingest={} action={} ampsConnection={} ampsTopic={} filter={}",
        ingestName,
        existed ? "updated" : "registered",
        ampsConnectionName,
        ampsTopic,
        "/type = 'STATUS_SERVICE'");
    return ingestName;
  }

  private static SchemaModel statusAppSchema() {
    return SchemaRecord.fromRecord(
        DefinitionStatusApp.class,
        SchemaRecord.Options.builder()
            .withGroup("platform")
            .withName("status-app-events")
            .withNestingMode(SchemaRecord.NestingMode.FLATTEN)
            .withIncludeAmpsCommand(true)
            .withIncludeRecordClassName(true)
            .withIncludePayloadJson(true)
            .withSkipNestedClasses(true)
            .build());
  }

  private static SchemaModel statusServiceSchema() {
    return SchemaRecord.fromRecord(
        DefinitionStatusService.class,
        SchemaRecord.Options.builder()
            .withGroup("platform")
            .withName("status-service-events")
            .withNestingMode(SchemaRecord.NestingMode.FLATTEN)
            .withIncludeAmpsCommand(true)
            .withIncludeRecordClassName(true)
            .withIncludePayloadJson(true)
            .withSkipNestedClasses(true)
            .build());
  }

  private static String transformStatusPayload(String payloadText, Integer ampsCommand) {
    String payload = Strings.requireNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(payloadText), "payloadText");
    try {
      JsonNode root = MAPPER.readTree(payload);
      boolean serviceStatus = "STATUS_SERVICE".equalsIgnoreCase(readStatusType(root));
      if (!serviceStatus && "RUNNING".equalsIgnoreCase(readStatusState(root))) {
        return null;
      }
      SchemaModel schema =
          serviceStatus ? STATUS_SERVICE_SCHEMA : STATUS_APP_SCHEMA;
      String recordClassName =
          serviceStatus ? STATUS_SERVICE_RECORD_CLASS : STATUS_APP_RECORD_CLASS;
      return SchemaRecordTransformer.transform(
          MAPPER,
          root,
          root,
          payload,
          ampsCommand,
          schema,
          recordClassName,
          SKIP_SOW_REPLAY);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to transform status payload: "
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(ex.getMessage(), "unknown"),
          ex);
    }
  }

  private static String readStatusType(JsonNode root) {
    if (root == null || root.isMissingNode()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode type = root.get("type");
    if (type != null && !type.isNull()) {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(type.asText(null));
      if (value != null) {
        return value;
      }
    }
    JsonNode envelope = root.path("envelope");
    if (!envelope.isObject()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode envelopeType = envelope.get("type");
    if (envelopeType == null || envelopeType.isNull()) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(envelopeType.asText(null));
  }

  private static String readStatusState(JsonNode root) {
    if (root == null || root.isMissingNode()) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode state = root.get("state");
    if (state == null || state.isNull()) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(state.asText(null));
  }
}



org.pronzato.fabric.service.config

===== FILE: fabric-lite-services/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/service/config/ConfigService.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.service.config;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.DiscoveryUrl;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceHandle;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.engine.ConfigEngine;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class ConfigService {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ConfigService.class);

  private ConfigService() {}

  public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
    Fabric.Session session = Fabric.newSession()
                              .withGroup("lab")
                              .withName("config")
                              .withDiscoveryUrls(DiscoveryUrl.URL)
                              .withKerberosKeytab(Path.of("vault/kerberos/lenny.keytab"))
                              .withKerberosUsername("lenny")
                              .build();
    try (session) {
      session.start();
      ServiceRunOptions options =
          ServiceRunOptions.builder()
              .withTlsCertChain(Path.of("vault", "tls", "demo-service.pem"))
              .withTlsPrivateKey(Path.of("vault", "tls", "demo-service.key"))
              .build();
      try (ServiceHandle service =
          session
              .services()
              .start("config", options, new ConfigEngine(session))) {
        LOGGER.info("[ConfigService] started name=config port={}", service.port());
        service.blockUntilShutdown();
      }
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.engine;

import io.grpc.Status;
import io.grpc.StatusException;
import io.grpc.StatusRuntimeException;
import io.grpc.stub.ServerCallStreamObserver;
import io.grpc.stub.StreamObserver;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigDecoder;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigAdmin;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigLineage;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.FabricConfigServiceGrpc;

import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.LineageResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListConfigsRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListConfigsResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListLayersRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListLayersResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListWorkflowsRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ListWorkflowsResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ResolveAtRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ResolveRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ResolveResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.SubscribeRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.UpdateRequestMessage;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.UpdateResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.WorkflowStatusMessage;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class ConfigEngine extends FabricConfigServiceGrpc.FabricConfigServiceImplBase {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ConfigEngine.class);
  private static final String OP_LIST_CONFIGS = "ListConfigs";
  private static final String OP_LIST_LAYERS = "ListLayers";
  private static final String OP_RESOLVE = "Resolve";
  private static final String OP_RESOLVE_AT = "ResolveAt";
  private static final String OP_LINEAGE = "Lineage";
  private static final String OP_LINEAGE_AT = "LineageAt";
  private static final String OP_GENERATE = "Generate";
  private static final String OP_SUBSCRIBE = "Subscribe";
  private static final String OP_LIST_WORKFLOWS = "ListWorkflows";
  private static final String OP_UPDATE = "Update";
  private static final String OP_APPROVE_AND_PUBLISH = "ApproveAndPublish";
  private static final String OP_REJECT = "Reject";
  private static final String OP_CANCEL = "Cancel";

  private final ConfigManager configManager;
  private final ConfigAdmin configAdmin;
  private final ConfigMapper mapper;

  public ConfigEngine(Fabric.Session session) {
    this(requireSession(session).configs());
  }

  public ConfigEngine(ConfigManager configManager) {
    this.configManager = Objects.requireNonNull(configManager, "configManager");
    this.configAdmin = Objects.requireNonNull(configManager.admin(), "configAdmin");
    this.mapper = new ConfigMapper();
  }

  @Override
  public void listConfigs(ListConfigsRequest request, StreamObserver<ListConfigsResponse> responseObserver) {
    unary(
        OP_LIST_CONFIGS,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          ListConfigsResponse.Builder builder = ListConfigsResponse.newBuilder();
          List<org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigInfo> configs = configManager.listConfigs();
          if (configs != null && !configs.isEmpty()) {
            for (org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigInfo info : configs) {
              builder.addConfigs(mapper.toProto(info));
            }
          }
          return builder.build();
        });
  }

  @Override
  public void listLayers(ListLayersRequest request, StreamObserver<ListLayersResponse> responseObserver) {
    unary(
        OP_LIST_LAYERS,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          String configId = requireNonBlank(request.getConfigId(), "configId");
          ListLayersResponse.Builder builder = ListLayersResponse.newBuilder();
          List<String> layers = configManager.listLayers(configId);
          if (layers != null && !layers.isEmpty()) {
            builder.addAllLayerIds(layers);
          }
          return builder.build();
        });
  }

  @Override
  public void resolve(ResolveRequest request, StreamObserver<ResolveResponse> responseObserver) {
    unary(
        OP_RESOLVE,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          String configId = requireNonBlank(request.getConfigId(), "configId");
          String layerId = requireNonBlank(request.getLayerId(), "layerId");
          JsonNode payload = configManager.resolve(configId, layerId, ConfigDecoder.asJsonNode());
          return ResolveResponse.newBuilder().setPayload(mapper.toStruct(payload)).build();
        });
  }

  @Override
  public void resolveAt(ResolveAtRequest request, StreamObserver<ResolveResponse> responseObserver) {
    unary(
        OP_RESOLVE_AT,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          String configId = requireNonBlank(request.getConfigId(), "configId");
          String layerId = requireNonBlank(request.getLayerId(), "layerId");
          Instant at = requireInstant(request.hasAtUtc(), request.getAtUtc(), "atUtc");
          JsonNode payload =
              configManager.resolveAt(configId, layerId, at, ConfigDecoder.asJsonNode());
          return ResolveResponse.newBuilder().setPayload(mapper.toStruct(payload)).build();
        });
  }

  @Override
  public void lineage(ResolveRequest request, StreamObserver<LineageResponse> responseObserver) {
    unary(
        OP_LINEAGE,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          String configId = requireNonBlank(request.getConfigId(), "configId");
          String layerId = requireNonBlank(request.getLayerId(), "layerId");
          ConfigLineage lineage = configManager.lineage(configId, layerId);
          LineageResponse.Builder builder = LineageResponse.newBuilder();
          org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigLineage protoLineage = mapper.toProto(lineage);
          if (protoLineage != null) {
            builder.setLineage(protoLineage);
          }
          return builder.build();
        });
  }

  @Override
  public void lineageAt(ResolveAtRequest request, StreamObserver<LineageResponse> responseObserver) {
    unary(
        OP_LINEAGE_AT,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          String configId = requireNonBlank(request.getConfigId(), "configId");
          String layerId = requireNonBlank(request.getLayerId(), "layerId");
          Instant at = requireInstant(request.hasAtUtc(), request.getAtUtc(), "atUtc");
          ConfigLineage lineage = configManager.lineageAt(configId, layerId, at);
          LineageResponse.Builder builder = LineageResponse.newBuilder();
          org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigLineage protoLineage = mapper.toProto(lineage);
          if (protoLineage != null) {
            builder.setLineage(protoLineage);
          }
          return builder.build();
        });
  }

  @Override
  public void generate(GenerateRequest request, StreamObserver<GenerateResponse> responseObserver) {
    unary(
        OP_GENERATE,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          String configId = requireNonBlank(request.getConfigId(), "configId");
          String layerId = requireNonBlank(request.getLayerId(), "layerId");
          ConfigManager.Language language = mapper.toModel(request.getLanguage());
          String base = Strings.trimToNull(request.getBasePackageOrModule());
          org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigCodegen generated =
              configManager.generate(configId, layerId, language, base);
          return GenerateResponse.newBuilder().setCodegen(mapper.toProto(generated)).build();
        });
  }

  @Override
  public void subscribe(SubscribeRequest request, StreamObserver<org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigUpdate> responseObserver) {
    String configId;
    String layerId;
    try {
      configId = requireNonBlank(request.getConfigId(), "configId");
      layerId = requireNonBlank(request.getLayerId(), "layerId");
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      responseObserver.onError(toStatusException(OP_SUBSCRIBE, ex));
      return;
    }

    AtomicBoolean closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);
    AtomicReference<ConfigSubscription> subscriptionRef = new AtomicReference<>();
    Object streamLock = new Object();
    Runnable closeSubscription =
        () -> {
          if (!closed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
            return;
          }
          ConfigSubscription subscription = subscriptionRef.getAndSet(null);
          if (subscription != null) {
            try {
              subscription.close();
            } catch (Exception ex) {
              LOGGER.warn("[ConfigService][{}] close failed: {}", OP_SUBSCRIBE, ex.toString());
            }
          }
        };

    if (responseObserver instanceof ServerCallStreamObserver<?>) {
      @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
      ServerCallStreamObserver<org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigUpdate> serverObserver =
          (ServerCallStreamObserver<org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigUpdate>) responseObserver;
      serverObserver.setOnCancelHandler(closeSubscription);
    }

    try {
      ConfigSubscription subscription =
          configManager.subscribe(
              configId,
              layerId,
              update -> {
                if (closed.get()) {
                  return;
                }
                try {
                  ConfigResolved resolved = null;
                  try {
                    JsonNode payload =
                        configManager.resolve(
                            update.configName(), update.layerId(), ConfigDecoder.asJsonNode());
                    ConfigLineage lineage = configManager.lineage(update.configName(), update.layerId());
                    resolved =
                        new ConfigResolved(
                            update.configName(),
                            update.layerId(),
                            payload,
                            update.updatedTimeUtc(),
                            null,
                            lineage);
                  } catch (Exception lineageError) {
                    LOGGER.warn(
                        "[ConfigService][{}] resolve/lineage failed configId={} layerId={} message={}",
                        OP_SUBSCRIBE,
                        update.configName(),
                        update.layerId(),
                        lineageError.getMessage());
                  }
                  org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigUpdate message =
                      mapper.toProto(update, resolved);
                  synchronized (streamLock) {
                    if (!closed.get()) {
                      responseObserver.onNext(message);
                    }
                  }
                } catch (Exception ex) {
                  synchronized (streamLock) {
                    if (!closed.get()) {
                      closeSubscription.run();
                      responseObserver.onError(toStatusException(OP_SUBSCRIBE, ex));
                    }
                  }
                }
              });
      subscriptionRef.set(subscription);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      closeSubscription.run();
      responseObserver.onError(toStatusException(OP_SUBSCRIBE, ex));
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void listWorkflows(
      ListWorkflowsRequest request, StreamObserver<ListWorkflowsResponse> responseObserver) {
    unary(
        OP_LIST_WORKFLOWS,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          int auditLimit = request.getAuditLimit();
          List<ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus> workflows =
              auditLimit > 0 ? configAdmin.list(auditLimit) : configAdmin.list();
          ListWorkflowsResponse.Builder builder = ListWorkflowsResponse.newBuilder();
          if (workflows != null && !workflows.isEmpty()) {
            for (ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus workflow : workflows) {
              builder.addWorkflows(mapper.toProto(workflow));
            }
          }
          return builder.build();
        });
  }

  @Override
  public void update(UpdateRequestMessage request, StreamObserver<UpdateResponse> responseObserver) {
    unary(
        OP_UPDATE,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          if (!request.hasRequest()) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("request is required");
          }
          ConfigAdmin.UpdateResult updated = configAdmin.update(mapper.toModel(request.getRequest()));
          return UpdateResponse.newBuilder().setResult(mapper.toProto(updated)).build();
        });
  }

  @Override
  public void approveAndPublish(
      DecisionRequest request, StreamObserver<WorkflowStatusMessage> responseObserver) {
    decision(OP_APPROVE_AND_PUBLISH, request, responseObserver, configAdmin::approveAndPublish);
  }

  @Override
  public void reject(DecisionRequest request, StreamObserver<WorkflowStatusMessage> responseObserver) {
    decision(OP_REJECT, request, responseObserver, configAdmin::reject);
  }

  @Override
  public void cancel(DecisionRequest request, StreamObserver<WorkflowStatusMessage> responseObserver) {
    decision(OP_CANCEL, request, responseObserver, configAdmin::cancel);
  }

  private void decision(
      String operation,
      DecisionRequest request,
      StreamObserver<WorkflowStatusMessage> responseObserver,
      DecisionHandler handler) {
    unary(
        operation,
        responseObserver,
        () -> {
          String configId = requireNonBlank(request.getConfigId(), "configId");
          String layerId = requireNonBlank(request.getLayerId(), "layerId");
          String comment = Strings.trimToNull(request.getComment());
          String subject = Strings.trimToNull(request.getSubject());
          ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus workflow = handler.apply(configId, layerId, comment, subject);
          return WorkflowStatusMessage.newBuilder().setWorkflow(mapper.toProto(workflow)).build();
        });
  }

  private <T> void unary(
      String operation, StreamObserver<T> responseObserver, ThrowingSupplier<T> supplier) {
    try {
      T response = supplier.get();
      responseObserver.onNext(response);
      responseObserver.onCompleted();
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      responseObserver.onError(toStatusException(operation, ex));
    }
  }

  private RuntimeException toStatusException(String operation, Throwable error) {
    Throwable cause = unwrap(error);
    if (cause instanceof StatusRuntimeException statusRuntimeException) {
      return statusRuntimeException;
    }
    if (cause instanceof StatusException statusException) {
      return statusException.getStatus().asRuntimeException();
    }
    String message = normalizeMessage(cause);
    Status status;
    if (isUnauthenticated(cause, message)) {
      status = Status.UNAUTHENTICATED;
    } else if (isPermissionDenied(cause, message)) {
      status = Status.PERMISSION_DENIED;
    } else if (isNotFound(cause, message)) {
      status = Status.NOT_FOUND;
    } else if (isFailedPrecondition(cause, message)) {
      status = Status.FAILED_PRECONDITION;
    } else if (cause instanceof IllegalArgumentException) {
      status = Status.INVALID_ARGUMENT;
    } else {
      status = Status.INTERNAL;
    }
    return status
        .withDescription(operation + ": " + message)
        .withCause(cause)
        .asRuntimeException();
  }

  private static Throwable unwrap(Throwable error) {
    if (error == null) {
      return new IllegalStateException("unknown failure");
    }
    Throwable current = error;
    while (current.getCause() != null
        && current != current.getCause()
        && !(current instanceof IllegalArgumentException)
        && !(current instanceof IllegalStateException)
        && !(current instanceof StatusRuntimeException)
        && !(current instanceof StatusException)) {
      current = current.getCause();
    }
    return current;
  }

  private static String normalizeMessage(Throwable error) {
    if (error == null) {
      return "unknown error";
    }
    String message = Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage());
    return message == null ? error.getClass().getSimpleName() : message;
  }

  private static boolean isNotFound(Throwable error, String message) {
    String type = error == null ? "" : error.getClass().getSimpleName();
    if (type.contains("NotFound")) {
      return true;
    }
    String lower = Strings.trimToEmpty(message).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return lower.contains("not found");
  }

  private static boolean isFailedPrecondition(Throwable error, String message) {
    String type = error == null ? "" : error.getClass().getSimpleName();
    if (type.contains("WorkflowStateException")) {
      return true;
    }
    String lower = Strings.trimToEmpty(message).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return lower.contains("config_chain_")
        || lower.contains("requires approved")
        || lower.contains("not allowed from")
        || lower.contains("pending scheduled publish")
        || lower.contains("scheduled publish is already effective");
  }

  private static boolean isPermissionDenied(Throwable error, String message) {
    if (error instanceof SecurityException) {
      return true;
    }
    String lower = Strings.trimToEmpty(message).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return lower.contains("permission denied") || lower.contains("access denied");
  }

  private static boolean isUnauthenticated(Throwable error, String message) {
    String lower = Strings.trimToEmpty(message).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return lower.contains("unauthenticated") || lower.contains("authentication");
  }

  private static Instant requireInstant(boolean present, com.google.protobuf.Timestamp value, String field) {
    if (!present) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(field + " is required");
    }
    return Instant.ofEpochSecond(value.getSeconds(), value.getNanos());
  }

  private static String requireNonBlank(String value, String field) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(field + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static Fabric.Session requireSession(Fabric.Session session) {
    return Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session");
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  private interface ThrowingSupplier<T> {
    T get() throws Exception;
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  private interface DecisionHandler {
    ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus apply(String configId, String layerId, String comment, String subject);
  }
}
