package org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.engine;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ArrayNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.JsonNodeFactory;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import com.google.protobuf.ByteString;
import com.google.protobuf.ListValue;
import com.google.protobuf.NullValue;
import com.google.protobuf.Struct;
import com.google.protobuf.Timestamp;
import com.google.protobuf.Value;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigAdmin;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigCodegen;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigInfo;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.ConfigManager.ConfigLineage;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.model.ConfigResolved;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.AuditEvent;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ChangeMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ChangeState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigUpdate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.DecisionAction;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.EffectiveEntry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.Language;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.PublishedConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.UpdateRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.UpdateResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.WorkflowStatus;

final class ConfigMapper {
  private final ObjectMapper mapper;

  ConfigMapper() {
    this(DiscoveryCodec.mapper());
  }

  ConfigMapper(ObjectMapper mapper) {
    this.mapper = Objects.requireNonNull(mapper, "mapper");
  }

  org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigInfo toProto(ConfigInfo info) {
    if (info == null) {
      return org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigInfo.getDefaultInstance();
    }
    return org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigInfo.newBuilder()
        .setConfigId(Strings.trimToEmpty(info.configId()))
        .setDisplayName(Strings.trimToEmpty(info.displayName()))
        .setSchemaKey(Strings.trimToEmpty(info.schemaKey()))
        .build();
  }

  Struct toStruct(Object payload) {
    if (payload == null) {
      return Struct.getDefaultInstance();
    }
    JsonNode node = mapper.valueToTree(payload);
    return toStruct(node);
  }

  Struct toStruct(JsonNode payload) {
    JsonNode node = payload == null ? null : payload;
    if (node == null || node.isNull()) {
      return Struct.getDefaultInstance();
    }
    if (!node.isObject()) {
      ObjectNode wrapped = mapper.createObjectNode();
      wrapped.set("value", node);
      node = wrapped;
    }
    Struct.Builder builder = Struct.newBuilder();
    node.fields()
        .forEachRemaining(
            field -> builder.putFields(field.getKey(), toValue(field.getValue())));
    return builder.build();
  }

  ObjectNode toObjectNode(Struct payload) {
    ObjectNode objectNode = mapper.createObjectNode();
    if (payload == null) {
      return objectNode;
    }
    payload
        .getFieldsMap()
        .forEach((key, value) -> objectNode.set(key, toJsonNode(value)));
    return objectNode;
  }

  org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigResolved toProto(ConfigResolved resolved) {
    if (resolved == null) {
      return org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigResolved.getDefaultInstance();
    }
    org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigResolved.Builder builder =
        org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigResolved.newBuilder()
            .setConfigId(Strings.trimToEmpty(resolved.configId()))
            .setLayerId(Strings.trimToEmpty(resolved.layerId()))
            .setPayload(toStruct(resolved.payload()));
    Timestamp updated = toTimestamp(Strings.trimToNull(resolved.updatedTimeUtc()));
    if (updated != null) {
      builder.setUpdatedTimeUtc(updated);
    }
    if (resolved.sources() != null && !resolved.sources().isEmpty()) {
      builder.putAllSources(new LinkedHashMap<>(resolved.sources()));
    }
    org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigLineage lineage = toProto(resolved.lineage());
    if (lineage != null) {
      builder.setLineage(lineage);
    }
    return builder.build();
  }

  org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigLineage toProto(ConfigLineage lineage) {
    if (lineage == null) {
      return null;
    }
    org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigLineage.Builder builder =
        org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigLineage.newBuilder()
            .setBaseConfigId(Strings.trimToEmpty(lineage.baseConfigId()))
            .setChainDepth(lineage.chainDepth())
            .setChainValid(lineage.chainValid())
            .setPayloadHash(Strings.trimToEmpty(lineage.payloadHash()))
            .setEffectiveTreeHash(Strings.trimToEmpty(lineage.effectiveTreeHash()))
            .setEffectiveTreeHashVersion(Strings.trimToEmpty(lineage.effectiveTreeHashVersion()));
    if (lineage.resolvedNodeIds() != null && !lineage.resolvedNodeIds().isEmpty()) {
      builder.addAllResolvedNodeIds(lineage.resolvedNodeIds());
    }
    if (lineage.resolvedLayers() != null && !lineage.resolvedLayers().isEmpty()) {
      builder.addAllResolvedLayers(lineage.resolvedLayers());
    }
    return builder.build();
  }

  org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigCodegen toProto(ConfigCodegen codegen) {
    if (codegen == null) {
      return org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigCodegen.getDefaultInstance();
    }
    org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigCodegen.Builder builder =
        org.pronzato.fabric.service.config.grpc.ConfigCodegen.newBuilder()
            .setZipBytes(ByteString.copyFrom(codegen.zipBytes()))
            .setFilename(Strings.trimToEmpty(codegen.filename()));
    if (codegen.stats() != null && !codegen.stats().isEmpty()) {
      builder.putAllStats(new LinkedHashMap<>(codegen.stats()));
    }
    List<String> generated = codegen.autogenCode();
    if (generated != null && !generated.isEmpty()) {
      builder.addAllGeneratedCode(generated);
    }
    return builder.build();
  }

  WorkflowStatus toProto(ConfigAdmin.WorkflowStatus workflow) {
    if (workflow == null) {
      return WorkflowStatus.getDefaultInstance();
    }
    WorkflowStatus.Builder builder =
        WorkflowStatus.newBuilder()

  private Value toValue(JsonNode value) {
    if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
      return Value.newBuilder().setNullValue(NullValue.NULL_VALUE).build();
    }
    if (value.isObject()) {
      return Value.newBuilder().setStructValue(toStruct(value)).build();
    }
    if (value.isArray()) {
      ListValue.Builder builder = ListValue.newBuilder();
      for (JsonNode item : value) {
        builder.addValues(toValue(item));
      }
      return Value.newBuilder().setListValue(builder).build();
    }
    if (value.isBoolean()) {
      return Value.newBuilder().setBoolValue(value.booleanValue()).build();
    }
    if (value.isNumber()) {
      return Value.newBuilder().setNumberValue(value.doubleValue()).build();
    }
    return Value.newBuilder().setStringValue(value.asText()).build();
  }

  private JsonNode toJsonNode(Value value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return JsonNodeFactory.instance.nullNode();
    }
    return switch (value.getKindCase()) {
      case NULL_VALUE, KIND_NOT_SET -> JsonNodeFactory.instance.nullNode();
      case BOOL_VALUE -> JsonNodeFactory.instance.booleanNode(value.getBoolValue());
      case NUMBER_VALUE -> JsonNodeFactory.instance.numberNode(value.getNumberValue());
      case STRING_VALUE -> JsonNodeFactory.instance.textNode(value.getStringValue());
      case STRUCT_VALUE -> toObjectNode(value.getStructValue());
      case LIST_VALUE -> toArrayNode(value.getListValue());
    };
  }

  private ArrayNode toArrayNode(ListValue listValue) {
    ArrayNode array = mapper.createArrayNode();
    if (listValue == null || listValue.getValuesCount() == 0) {
      return array;
    }
    for (Value value : listValue.getValuesList()) {
      array.add(toJsonNode(value));
    }
    return array;
  }

  private static String text(JsonNode node, String fieldName) {
    if (node == null || fieldName == null) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode field = node.get(fieldName);
    return field == null || field.isNull() ? null : Strings.trimToNull(field.asText());
  }

  private static final int METHODID_LIST_CONFIGS = 0;
  private static final int METHODID_LIST_LAYERS = 1;
  private static final int METHODID_RESOLVE = 2;
  private static final int METHODID_RESOLVE_AT = 3;
  private static final int METHODID_LINEAGE = 4;
  private static final int METHODID_LINEAGE_AT = 5;
  private static final int METHODID_GENERATE = 6;
  private static final int METHODID_SUBSCRIBE = 7;
  private static final int METHODID_LIST_WORKFLOWS = 8;
  private static final int METHODID_UPDATE = 9;
  private static final int METHODID_APPROVE_AND_PUBLISH = 10;
  private static final int METHODID_REJECT = 11;
  private static final int METHODID_CANCEL = 12;

  private static final class MethodHandlers<Req, Resp> implements
      io.grpc.stub.ServerCalls.UnaryMethod<Req, Resp>,
      io.grpc.stub.ServerCalls.ServerStreamingMethod<Req, Resp>,
      io.grpc.stub.ServerCalls.ClientStreamingMethod<Req, Resp>,
      io.grpc.stub.ServerCalls.BidiStreamingMethod<Req, Resp> {
    private final AsyncService serviceImpl;
    private final int methodId;

    MethodHandlers(AsyncService serviceImpl, int methodId) {
      this.serviceImpl = serviceImpl;
      this.methodId = methodId;
    }

    @java.lang.Override
    @java.lang.SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
